        }

          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;

          flex-wrap: no-wrap;

        }

        }

            width: 100%;

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





It seems to be a torque issue in v8, but I don't have a full root cause analysis. However, I have written an exploit in old version chrome and provided the poc.



<span class="line"><!---->It seems to be a torque issue in v8, but I don't have a full root cause analysis. However, I have written an exploit in old version chrome and provided the poc.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





VERSION



<b class="line"><!---->VERSION<!----></b>



<br>





Tested on v8 version 10.9.0(latest version), introduced on v8 version 8.6



<span class="line"><!---->Tested on v8 version 10.9.0(latest version), introduced on v8 version 8.6<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





REPRODUCTION CASE



<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>



<br>





- poc



<span class="line"><!---->- poc<!----></span>



<br>





    - Download the latest version v8 10.9.0



<span class="line"><!---->    - Download the latest version v8 10.9.0<!----></span>



<br>





    - ./d8 poc.js, and will leak hole.



<span class="line"><!---->    - ./d8 poc.js, and will leak hole.<!----></span>



<br>





- exploit



<span class="line"><!---->- exploit<!----></span>



<br>





    - leak hole is a powerful primitive.



<span class="line"><!---->    - leak hole is a powerful primitive.<!----></span>



<br>





    For example in the wild vulnerability: 



<span class="line"><!---->    For example in the wild vulnerability: <!----></span>





https://bugs.chromium.org/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1315901,It



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://bugs.chromium.org/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1315901,It"><!---->https://bugs.chromium.org/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1315901,It<!----></a>





 use the above primitive to exploit the vulnerability.



<span class="line"><!----> use the above primitive to exploit the vulnerability.<!----></span>



<br>





    I have written the exploit with v8 9.7.106.19 in the same way, and although this exploit is not available in the latest version, it still demonstrates the high exploitability of this vulnerability.



<span class="line"><!---->    I have written the exploit with v8 9.7.106.19 in the same way, and although this exploit is not available in the latest version, it still demonstrates the high exploitability of this vulnerability.<!----></span>



<br>





    - Written in v8 9.7.106.19, compiled via `tools/dev/gm.py x64.release`,



<span class="line"><!---->    - Written in v8 9.7.106.19, compiled via `tools/dev/gm.py x64.release`,<!----></span>



<br>





    - ./d8 exp.js, the calculator will pop up.



<span class="line"><!---->    - ./d8 exp.js, the calculator will pop up.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





FOR CRASHES, PLEASE INCLUDE THE FOLLOWING ADDITIONAL INFORMATION



<b class="line"><!---->FOR CRASHES, PLEASE INCLUDE THE FOLLOWING ADDITIONAL INFORMATION<!----></b>



<br>





Type of crash: tab



<span class="line"><!---->Type of crash: tab<!----></span>

syg@chromium.org

<div class="issue-diff">
        <!---->
          <strong><!---->Status:</strong>
          
          Started
          (was: Unconfirmed)
          <br>
        <!---->

Root cause analysis is as follows.



<span class="line"><!---->Root cause analysis is as follows.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Background



<span class="line"><!---->Background<!----></span>



<br>





==========



<span class="line"><!---->==========<!----></span>



<br>





Promise.any(iterable) [1] is a promise combinator that iterates all promises in the iterable arguments, combining them, using the "then" function, into a new promise that resolves if any input promise resolves and rejects if all input promises are rejected.



<span class="line"><!---->Promise.any(iterable) [1] is a promise combinator that iterates all promises in the iterable arguments, combining them, using the "then" function, into a new promise that resolves if any input promise resolves and rejects if all input promises are rejected.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Bug



<span class="line"><!---->Bug<!----></span>



<br>





===



<span class="line"><!---->===<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





1. Promise.any handles builtin subclassing by treating its receiver as a constructor to be used to construct the promise to be returned. A user function can be passed with an overridden "then" method that synchronously resolves or rejects.



<span class="line"><!---->1. Promise.any handles builtin subclassing by treating its receiver as a constructor to be used to construct the promise to be returned. A user function can be passed with an overridden "then" method that synchronously resolves or rejects.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





2. During iteration, the variable remainingElementsCount counts how many input promises there are. Recall the behavior of Promise.any is to reject the combined promise if all input promises are rejected. This variable is closed over by the reject handler: if the count == 0, then the combined promise is rejected [2].



<span class="line"><!---->2. During iteration, the variable remainingElementsCount counts how many input promises there are. Recall the behavior of Promise.any is to reject the combined promise if all input promises are rejected. This variable is closed over by the reject handler: if the count == 0, then the combined promise is rejected [2].<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





3. remainingElementsCount is initialized to 1 (not 0!) so that if the first input promise that is synchronously rejected during iteration does not incorrectly reject the combined promise. (Since the input is an iterable, the number of input promises is unknown ahead of time.) Each iteration increments remainingElementsCount by 1. At the end of iteration, remainingElementsCount is decremented by 1.



<span class="line"><!---->3. remainingElementsCount is initialized to 1 (not 0!) so that if the first input promise that is synchronously rejected during iteration does not incorrectly reject the combined promise. (Since the input is an iterable, the number of input promises is unknown ahead of time.) Each iteration increments remainingElementsCount by 1. At the end of iteration, remainingElementsCount is decremented by 1.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





4. When the combined promise is rejected, it is rejected with an AggregateError, which in turn contains an array of values for each input promise rejection. V8's implementation of Promise.any lazily constructs this errors array.



<span class="line"><!---->4. When the combined promise is rejected, it is rejected with an AggregateError, which in turn contains an array of values for each input promise rejection. V8's implementation of Promise.any lazily constructs this errors array.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The V8 bug is in (4). The new capacity of errors array is incorrectly computed as the max(remainingElementsCount, index of the input promise + 1). Because remainingElementsCount is 1 higher than the true value during iteration of the input, synchronous rejection creates an errors array that is 1 element bigger. This element is never assigned to and remains the uninitialized TheHole value, which leaks to user script.



<span class="line"><!---->The V8 bug is in (4). The new capacity of errors array is incorrectly computed as the max(remainingElementsCount, index of the input promise + 1). Because remainingElementsCount is 1 higher than the true value during iteration of the input, synchronous rejection creates an errors array that is 1 element bigger. This element is never assigned to and remains the uninitialized TheHole value, which leaks to user script.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Fix up at 



<span class="line"><!---->Fix up at <!----></span>





https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/v8/v8/+/3988924



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/v8/v8/+/3988924"><!---->https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/v8/v8/+/3988924<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





[1] 



<span class="line"><!---->[1] <!----></span>





https://tc39.es/ecma262/#sec-promise.any



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://tc39.es/ecma262/#sec-promise.any"><!---->https://tc39.es/ecma262/#sec-promise.any<!----></a>



<br>





[2] 



<span class="line"><!---->[2] <!----></span>





https://tc39.es/ecma262/#sec-promise.any-reject-element-functions



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://tc39.es/ecma262/#sec-promise.any-reject-element-functions"><!---->https://tc39.es/ecma262/#sec-promise.any-reject-element-functions<!----></a>





 step 10



<span class="line"><!----> step 10<!----></span>

[Promise.any] Fix errors allocation



<span class="line"><!---->[Promise.any] Fix errors allocation<!----></span>



<br>

Another great find! While the exploit uses the "Map.prototype.delete technique" which no longer works on current Chrome [1], we should assume that leaking TheHole can be exploited in other ways as well. Setting the severity accordingly.

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {
          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
          text-decoration: underline;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container td {
          padding: 0.25em 8px;
          white-space: nowrap;
        }
        .screenreader-hidden {
          clip: rect(1px, 1px, 1px, 1px);
          height: 1px;
          overflow: hidden;
          position: absolute;
          white-space: nowrap;
          width: 1px;
        }
